# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Java Dependency Injection with Kafka Plugin Architecture

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the plugin/extension loading system: the PluginClassLoader, the plugin scanning via reflection, and the interface-based dependency injection used for Connector, Converter, and HeaderConverter plugins.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Perfect! I've successfully completed the comprehensive analysis and created the `/workspace/answer.json` file. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary: Java Plugin/Extension Loading System in Apache Kafka

I've identified **47 Java source files** that implement Kafka's sophisticated plugin/extension loading system, organized into several key subsystems:

### **Core Plugin Isolation (5 files)**
- **PluginClassLoader**: Custom URLClassLoader with child-first classloading for plugin isolation
- **DelegatingClassLoader**: Parent classloader that delegates to isolated plugin classloaders
- **ClassLoaderFactory/PluginClassLoaderFactory**: Factories for creating classloader instances
- **LoaderSwap**: Thread context classloader management utility

### **Plugin Discovery System (5 files)**
- **PluginScanner**: Abstract base for plugin discovery
- **ReflectionScanner**: Uses ClassGraph for comprehensive runtime reflection-based scanning
- **ServiceLoaderScanner**: Uses Java ServiceLoader mechanism with META-INF manifests
- **PluginUtils**: Utility functions for plugin source management
- **PluginDiscoveryMode**: Configuration for hybrid discovery behavior

### **Plugin Metadata & Types (5 files)**
- **PluginType**: Enumeration of 9 plugin categories (Source, Sink, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, RestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy)
- **PluginDesc**: Generic descriptor holding plugin class, version, type, and classloader
- **PluginSource**: Record representing plugin source locations
- **PluginScanResult**: Aggregates discovery results by type

### **Core Plugin Interfaces (18 files)**
- **Connector interfaces**: Connector (base), SourceConnector, SinkConnector
- **Data transformation**: Converter, HeaderConverter, Trans

implements a comprehensive Java-based plugin/extension loading system in the Connect framework, centered around interface-based dependency injection and reflective plugin discovery.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Isolation System\\n\\nThe plugin isolation mechanism is built on three key classloader components:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first classloading semantics for plugin isolation. Each plugin gets loaded in its own classloader to prevent conflicts with shared dependencies.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A parent classloader that delegates to isolated PluginClassLoaders while maintaining child-first delegation for plugins. It manages a map of discovered plugins and their classloaders.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** and **PluginClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java and PluginClassLoaderFactory.java): Factories that create instances of these classloaders, with support for mocking in tests.\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery System\\n\\nThe system supports two plugin discovery mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Uses ClassGraph library to scan classpath for classes implementing plugin interfaces at runtime. This provides comprehensive discovery but has higher computational cost.\\n\\n2. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism with META-INF/services manifest files. Faster but requires explicit manifest entries.\\n\\nBoth scanners extend **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java), which provides the common discovery framework.\\n\\n## Plugin Type System\\n\\n**PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java) is an enumeration defining the plugin categories:\\n- SOURCE (SourceConnector)\\n- SINK (SinkConnector)\\n- CONVERTER (Converter)\\n- HEADER_CONVERTER (HeaderConverter)\\n- TRANSFORMATION (Transformation)\\n- PREDICATE (Predicate)\\n- CONFIGPROVIDER (ConfigProvider)\\n- REST_EXTENSION (ConnectRestExtension)\\n- CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY (ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy)\\n\\n## Plugin Metadata and Results\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): A generic descriptor class that holds metadata about a discovered plugin including class reference, version, type, and classloader.\\n\\n2. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Aggregates SortedSets of PluginDesc objects for each plugin type, representing the complete discovery result.\\n\\n3. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, JAR hierarchy, or class hierarchy) with its associated URLs and classloader.\\n\\n## Interface-Based Plugin System\\n\\nThe plugin system uses interface-based dependency injection for nine key plugin types:\\n\\n1. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base interface for connectors, with subclasses:\\n   - **SourceConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java)\\n   - **SinkConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java)\\n\\n2. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for converting between Kafka Connect data format and serialized bytes.\\n\\n3. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Specialized converter for Kafka message headers.\\n\\n4. **Transformation** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java): Generic interface for single message transformations.\\n\\n5. **Predicate** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java): Interface for predicates that determine when transformations apply.\\n\\n6. **ConfigProvider** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/provider/ConfigProvider.java): Interface for providing configuration data from external sources.\\n\\n7. **ConnectRestExtension** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java): Interface for extending Connect REST API with custom resources.\\n\\n8. **ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java): Interface for enforcing policies on client config overrides.\\n\\n9. **Task** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Task.java): Base for SourceTask and SinkTask with associated record and context types.\\n\\n## Configuration and Dependency Injection\\n\\nAll plugins implement **Configurable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java), which provides a single configure(Map<String, ?>) method for dependency injection. Plugins may optionally implement **Monitorable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/metrics/Monitorable.java) to register custom metrics.\\n\\n## Plugin Instantiation and Classloader Management\\n\\n**Plugins** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) is the central manager that:\\n- Discovers and maintains plugin descriptors\\n- Instantiates plugins with appropriate classloaders\\n- Manages classloader context switching via **LoaderSwap** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java)\\n- Supports versioned plugin loading\\n- Provides plugin recommendations via **PluginsRecommenders** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java)\\n\\n## Utility and Infrastructure\\n\\n1. **PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java): Provides utilities for:\\n   - Creating PluginSource instances from plugin locations\\n   - Determining if classes should load in isolation\\n   - Plugin name and alias resolution\\n\\n2. **PluginDiscoveryMode** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDiscoveryMode.java): Enum controlling hybrid discovery behavior (ServiceLoader + Reflection combinations).\\n\\n3. **WorkerConfig** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/WorkerConfig.java): Configuration class defining plugin path and discovery mode settings.\\n\\n4. **ConnectMetrics** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/ConnectMetrics.java): Metrics wrapper for monitoring plugin behavior.\\n\\n## Discovery Tools\\n\\n**ConnectPluginPath** (tools/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/tools/ConnectPluginPath.java) and **ManifestWorkspace** (tools/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/tools/ManifestWorkspace.java) provide command-line tools for plugin discovery and ServiceLoader manifest synchronization.\\n\\nThis architecture provides a flexible, extensible plugin system with classloading isolation, support for multiple plugin discovery mechanisms, and interface-based dependency injection suitable for a distributed data integration platform.\"\n}\n",

\"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java\", \"symbol\": \"ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Apache Kafka implements a comprehensive Java-based plugin/extension loading system in the Connect framework, centered around interface-based dependency injection and reflective plugin discovery.\\n\\n## Core Plugin Isolation System\\n\\nThe plugin isolation mechanism is built on three key classloader components:\\n\\n1. **PluginClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginClassLoader.java): A custom URLClassLoader that implements child-first classloading semantics for plugin isolation. Each plugin gets loaded in its own classloader to prevent conflicts with shared dependencies.\\n\\n2. **DelegatingClassLoader** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/DelegatingClassLoader.java): A parent classloader that delegates to isolated PluginClassLoaders while maintaining child-first delegation for plugins. It manages a map of discovered plugins and their classloaders.\\n\\n3. **ClassLoaderFactory** and **PluginClassLoaderFactory** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ClassLoaderFactory.java and PluginClassLoaderFactory.java): Factories that create instances of these classloaders, with support for mocking in tests.\\n\\n## Plugin Discovery System\\n\\nThe system supports two plugin discovery mechanisms:\\n\\n1. **ReflectionScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ReflectionScanner.java): Uses ClassGraph library to scan classpath for classes implementing plugin interfaces at runtime. This provides comprehensive discovery but has higher computational cost.\\n\\n2. **ServiceLoaderScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/ServiceLoaderScanner.java): Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism with META-INF/services manifest files. Faster but requires explicit manifest entries.\\n\\nBoth scanners extend **PluginScanner** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanner.java), which provides the common discovery framework.\\n\\n## Plugin Type System\\n\\n**PluginType** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginType.java) is an enumeration defining the plugin categories:\\n- SOURCE (SourceConnector)\\n- SINK (SinkConnector)\\n- CONVERTER (Converter)\\n- HEADER_CONVERTER (HeaderConverter)\\n- TRANSFORMATION (Transformation)\\n- PREDICATE (Predicate)\\n- CONFIGPROVIDER (ConfigProvider)\\n- REST_EXTENSION (ConnectRestExtension)\\n- CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_OVERRIDE_POLICY (ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy)\\n\\n## Plugin Metadata and Results\\n\\n1. **PluginDesc** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDesc.java): A generic descriptor class that holds metadata about a discovered plugin including class reference, version, type, and classloader.\\n\\n2. **PluginScanResult** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginScanResult.java): Aggregates SortedSets of PluginDesc objects for each plugin type, representing the complete discovery result.\\n\\n3. **PluginSource** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginSource.java): A record representing a source location for plugins (classpath, single JAR, JAR hierarchy, or class hierarchy) with its associated URLs and classloader.\\n\\n## Interface-Based Plugin System\\n\\nThe plugin system uses interface-based dependency injection for nine key plugin types:\\n\\n1. **Connector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Connector.java): Base interface for connectors, with subclasses:\\n   - **SourceConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/source/SourceConnector.java)\\n   - **SinkConnector** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/sink/SinkConnector.java)\\n\\n2. **Converter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/Converter.java): Interface for converting between Kafka Connect data format and serialized bytes.\\n\\n3. **HeaderConverter** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/HeaderConverter.java): Specialized converter for Kafka message headers.\\n\\n4. **Transformation** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/Transformation.java): Generic interface for single message transformations.\\n\\n5. **Predicate** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/transforms/predicates/Predicate.java): Interface for predicates that determine when transformations apply.\\n\\n6. **ConfigProvider** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/provider/ConfigProvider.java): Interface for providing configuration data from external sources.\\n\\n7. **ConnectRestExtension** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/rest/ConnectRestExtension.java): Interface for extending Connect REST API with custom resources.\\n\\n8. **ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/policy/ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy.java): Interface for enforcing policies on client config overrides.\\n\\n9. **Task** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/connector/Task.java): Base for SourceTask and SinkTask with associated record and context types.\\n\\n## Configuration and Dependency Injection\\n\\nAll plugins implement **Configurable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/Configurable.java), which provides a single configure(Map<String, ?>) method for dependency injection. Plugins may optionally implement **Monitorable** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/metrics/Monitorable.java) to register custom metrics.\\n\\n## Plugin Instantiation and Classloader Management\\n\\n**Plugins** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/Plugins.java) is the central manager that:\\n- Discovers and maintains plugin descriptors\\n- Instantiates plugins with appropriate classloaders\\n- Manages classloader context switching via **LoaderSwap** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/LoaderSwap.java)\\n- Supports versioned plugin loading\\n- Provides plugin recommendations via **PluginsRecommenders** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginsRecommenders.java)\\n\\n## Utility and Infrastructure\\n\\n1. **PluginUtils** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginUtils.java): Provides utilities for:\\n   - Creating PluginSource instances from plugin locations\\n   - Determining if classes should load in isolation\\n   - Plugin name and alias resolution\\n\\n2. **PluginDiscoveryMode** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/PluginDiscoveryMode.java): Enum controlling hybrid discovery behavior (ServiceLoader + Reflection combinations).\\n\\n3. **WorkerConfig** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/WorkerConfig.java): Configuration class defining plugin path and discovery mode settings.\\n\\n4. **ConnectMetrics** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/ConnectMetrics.java): Metrics wrapper for monitoring plugin behavior.\\n\\n## Discovery Tools\\n\\n**ConnectPluginPath** (tools/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/tools/ConnectPluginPath.java) and **ManifestWorkspace** (tools/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/tools/ManifestWorkspace.java) provide command-line tools for plugin discovery and ServiceLoader manifest synchronization.\\n\\nThis architecture provides a flexible, extensible plugin system with classloading isolation, support for multiple plugin discovery mechanisms, and interface-based dependency injection suitable for a distributed data integration platform.\"\n}\n",
